Hannibal's Catering & Events has been catering lunches and dinners for my company for months now. Every day the staff is friendly and efficient. They have expressed outstanding service with exceptional cleanliness in regard to the current pandemic. Taylor is always shinning with her bubbly personality and over-the-top customer service. Every staff member is friendly and they don't mind a bit of banter while serving us. Although meals are contracted through work they never fail to remember my dietary needs and shield my plate from meat and dairy while offering amazing vegan options! 10 out of 10 I would recommend to a friend!< /review>

<Rate>1<//Rate><review>Absolute worst experience of my life. If you don't have a large event don't go with them. We had an 80 guest wedding and this wasn't a large account to them.
My email to our coordinator after the event is below. The company essentially called me a liar in their response and accepted no responsibility for the issues. I contacted them several times throughout the process with no response due to my coordinator having a medical issue. When my fiance finally called all they did was send an invoice without any of the information I requested.
I would advise you to seek another company if you want a smooth event on a lower budget- if your not forking out  10,000 they could care less.

I wanted to take a moment to share with you the experience we had with Hannibal's catering for our wedding this Saturday. We choose Hannibal's for the reputation and reviews, and we couldn't have had a worse experience. I understand you had a medical emergency that caused you to be out before our wedding. However, The company signed into a contract with us to provide a service for a wedding we did not receive. I am writing to explain to you the numerous issues that arose, and provide you with the opportunity to remedy the situation before further action is taken.

Timeline-
The caterers arrived at 4:30pm. Due to their tardiness, the appetizers were not set up until 45 minutes into our cocktail hour.. On top of that.. They were served ICE COLD, both the mini sliders and coconut shrimp skewers were not heated in any manner before being served to our guests.

"Bartender"-
We signed into a contract with Hannibal's to provide a bartender for the event. The employee you sent not only was not a bartender- she felt the need to tell every single guest that she was not a bartender and had never bar-tended before. She complained to all my guests, and told myself and my husband she wasn't a bartender. We had prepared mixed cocktails in advance so she only had to pour them and add the garnishments. She did not put a single garnishment on any drink even after being directed to do so multiple times. We purchased and prepared all the garnishments with our own money on our own time. Her negative attitude was a horrific experience for myself as the bride as I had multiple guests come up to me asking where she was from and why she didn't want to be there so badly.  My guests ended up making their own drinks to avoid her because she was rude to everyone.
Dinner-
I had emailed in advance asking what decorations we would need to provide for the dinner presentation and was told not to worry that was all part of the contract. There was absolutely no presentation. The food was all served in plain black trays with one flower arrangement on the table that didn't even match our color scheme. We would have provided our own setup if it would have been articulated that you guys were not going to put in any effort in arranging an attractive presentation for a wedding.  On top of all these issues, no where in the contract did it state the servers would take all the additional food. We had guests staying the night and a refrigerated area to store the food and the leftovers were taken without our consent.
Dessert-
Fortunately we had planned our own platters and decor for dessert which helped as there was no plan by your company to provide decor or presentation for this. The servers complained that we asked for the desserts to be put on our platters. We also ordered the 4 variety option and didn't receive the Russian tea cookies- which wasn't a huge deal for us but it was never communicated to us that all options would not be provided.< /review>< pics>

< Review>
The bronze Mechanics Monument was created by sculptor Douglas Tilden and dedicated in 1901.

Tilden was born in Chico, California, in 1860. At age four, he contracted scarlet fever which left him deaf and mute for life.

Tilden attended the California School for the Deaf and UC Berkeley, then he studied art in Paris.

The Mechanics Monument was commissioned to honor industrialist Peter Donahue, founder of the San Francisco & North Pacific Railroad.

The bronze depicts five men struggling to punch a hole through a metal plate with a punch press. At the base are symbols of Donahue's professions: an anvil represents foundries, a propeller represents shipping, and the driving wheel and connecting rod represent railroads.

When the monument was dedicated, many citizens were shocked by the sight of rude mechanicals cavorting in the street without their knickers. Editorials demanded that Tilden put trousers on the men, an interesting aesthetic and technical challenge. Tilden ignored the controversy and it faded away.< /Review>

It is where people went after the 1906earthquake, there to plan what to do next. The statue in question refers to the Mechanics Movement of the ,19th Century which gave us all our builders and hands-on people. It was an international movement with Libraries and Centers in most advanced towns and cities.<//Review>

<rate>4< /rate>< Text>
The new pho place just opened recently. We came here twice (both dinner time) and liked it very much. The interior is newly remodeled and beautiful. The pho broth is sweet and cinnamon-y than other pho places but I like it. We have tried several other dishes and liked them too. <rate>5<//rate><Review>Finding a good Pho restaurant in Little Saigon? Easy
Finding a good Pho restaurant anywhere else in OC? Hard

This is probably the best Pho restaurant in Tustin, and if it was in Little Saigon, it would probably get a cult following as well. Decor is very hip and modern. Oversized wood chairs and floor give the space a warm feel and lots of natural light brighten up the place.

The broth is packed with aromatics. The cinnamon & star anise are very pronounced. I feel the brisket could be more tender. They bring your utensils out in this neat little woven basket.

Only down side I've seen here is the slow service, especially during the lunch rush. It took 15 minutes to get our food out to us. That's an eternity when you're talking Vietnamese restaurant terms.

Overall, solid spot for Pho and I believe I'll keep returning.< /Review><Pics>None<//Pics>< response>

<Text>The environment of the place is really nice and comforting, i arrived and got seated right away but they did take long to take my order i want to say it was atleast 10min before i had to stare at the waiter and then he came and took my order. I did like that he mentioned the lunch special which was basically what i was ordering so that was nice . The broth its self tasted really bland to me, im not one to add sriracha or the "brown sauce" to my pho and i did to this one and i added quite alot. I got the chicken pho and to me even though the broth itself was boiling hot the chikens texture just seemed thick and dull. The lunch special came with 2 eggrolls and they actually forgot to bring them out to me, i had to remind the waiter that my order also came with eggrolls. I was upset with the eggrolls because they weren't hot they were warm but ive had eggrolls where they are still cooking on the plate. The only reason im not giving it a 1 star is because the pho was hot and it stayed hot till the moment i finished it and it didnt look thick like most pho get when they start to cool down. Would i come back , no i wouldn't . Would i recommend it to people? no, but the place was pretty packed with people but this is my opinon.</Text>< Pics>

<user_name>Carmen N< /user_name><date>1600465572145<//date><Rating>5<//Rating><review>This place has always been my favorite for chicken pho (pho ga). Their broth is very flavorful and the chicken is good quality as well as meaty! They give you the option to choose between white meat or dark meat. I also love that they automatically use the large flat noodles (banh lon) instead of the thin ones. That has always been my preference for noodles. Don't come here expecting top notch service because you won't get that anywhere in the Little Saigon area. Come for good food and a delicious dessert (che) that comes free of charge at the end of the meal. They also accept credit card as payment which is a huge bonus compared to other restaurants within the area. Overall, I've always really satisfied after my meals here. You really can't go wrong with their chicken pho!<//review>< Pictures>

<time>1617642557468<//time><Rate>1</Rate>< review>
Buyer beware! The longer you rent from Jefferson Self Storage the more you will pay! They advertise low prices to get you in the door, next thing you know your rates are being increased above the average yearly rate of inflation. I have been a loyal customer for two years now, never missed a payment and now I'm being charged $168 a month for a 10x10 drive up unit, non climate controlled, while a new customer can get the exact same unit right now for $145 a month. How is that fair? Beware of their cheaper prices, their units are mediocre, the light in my unit has been out for two years now and they have a major pest issue being right next to a vacant lot in the back.
**Update 4/5/2021 Found a rotting, dead rat in the corner of my storage unit upon clearing it out. Rat poop all love the place and rat poison trash left in my unit by Jefferson Self storage, see pictures below. This is absolutely un-satisfactory for paying $167 a month for a 10x10 drive up unit. On top of barely any security cameras, limited hours of use, and a major rodent infestation problem it's obvious this storage company is absorbing all of the profits from increasing rent every year and not updating their services and storage. So you and I, the consumer pay more but get the same below standard service in return.

<text>The Simple Greek was almost empty while the neighboring restaurants bustled with customers; I should have taken that as a sign that the 4-star Yelp average was misleading. But the menu sounded appealing, so I went in.

Even though no one else was dining in when I got there, I had to scout around for a table that had been cleaned of crumbs from previous diners.

I ordered a bowl with lentils as the base. The lentils looked like they'd formed a crust on top when he scooped them out of the warming pan; they'd probably been there for a while. I added falafel, some cucumber, olives, tomato, tzatziki and hummus. Overall it was just ok. The falafel didn't have that crispness with the steamy soft inside that a good, fresh one has. Maybe it had also been sitting too long. The taste of my dish wasn't bad, but it just didn't seem fresh or particularly appealing.

I also ordered the Greek Fries. They were ready right away, because the fries were already cooked, being kept in a container. Maybe they were being kept warm or maybe thrown in the microwave to reheat? They were oily and limp -- you know, the way fries get when they are overdone and turn translucent and brown. Feta cheese and some barely discernible oregano were sprinkled on top. I ate about a third of the fries before I realized they were giving me no pleasure in exchange for the calories, so the rest went in the bin.

Overall, The Simple Greek is not a place I'd come back to.<//text></record></dataset><record>

< Review>
I drive by this place every day on my way home from work so I thought I would give it a try. They had an ad for a BOGO on facebook for their Grand Opening so why not check it out. The staff was wonderful. Freddy was super polite,friendly and hilarious from beginning to end.

I ordered traditional gyro meat bowls with half lemon rice and salad and then added the feta,onion,garbanzo beans, cucumber and banana peppers with my sauces on the side. It also comes with your choice of white or wheat pita bread.

If you are not sure what sauces you will like the staff will give you samples of it to try. I sampled the tzatziki sauce as I am very picky about it and enjoyed it. I also really enjoyed the spicy red pepper sauce and greek dressing.

I know I definitely will be back :D</Review>

<Review>OK in pinch But definitely needs work.
As of November 2019, this is a brand New, small, fast food style Greek restaurant that's clean, and has decent parking.
New, young employees/staff are friendly, But definitely need more experience with food preparation and general cooking skills.
Similar to Chipotle style ordering, line up and choose your Basic Greek type menu items as they put together in front of you till you get to the register.
Ingredients are premade and generic. In my opinion, meats are not well seasoned and don't taste high quality, and the college kids meat cooking skills are questionable at best but at least appears to try.

< text>
I have had my rec since 2006 so I have seen my share of dispensaries.
I would have to say Changes ranks in the top five. The only reason I say top five ,for now, is because I have only been there once. Spoiler alert - I plan on returning.
My first trip there was for a special they had but they had closed a little early (15 minutes so not complaining). I went back because I have had several friends who have recommended them for concentrates. I got their Avocado Diamond Sauce. I would have to say its potency is right where I needed it as I have a high tolerance and it was a very smooth tasting draw. I will definitely being getting more of this line as it has been awhile since I have had an extract that got me excited.
Not only did they make sure I had all the information I needed about their products they also honored the deal I originally went in for the first time. Honoring the deal was a rare gesture these days so I very much appreciated it.
I would highly (no pun intended) recommend giving them a try as I believe you will make a second trip.
Stay Green.<//text>
